######x隶嘻赓渝祭x######
block GlobalTimerA > 28800 && Visitor >= 30
	SetVisitor0
	EndWindow 3211314

		#\n\nx仍户氏友\nx隶嘻互莽木切扎匀凶心凶中分方

########x旦正□矛伉伙及瑞kx########
block HaveLeak1item == 13600 && Visitor >= 1000 && Visitor < 2000
	Window 3211315,yes,no

		#\n\nx旦正□矛伉伙及瑞k匹掸董允月方z\nx巨生伙幼□医匹y100?手日丹仃升中中


	Window_yes gold < 100
		EndWindow 3211316

		#\n\nx云嗯互卅五扎y掸董匹五卅中方

	Window_yes Item 13600 >= 1
	LocalCount1 = Random 3,0
	killitem 13600
	AddGold -100
	if LocalCount1 == 1
		GiveLeak1Item (13601%60,13600%35,13604%5)
		EndWindow 3211317

		#\n\nx引凶yF化仁木方卅z
	else	
		if LocalCount1 == 2
			GiveLeak1Item (13601%30,13600%20,13640%10,13641%10,606200%10,606201%10,13644%5,606204%5)
			EndWindow 3211318

		#\n\nx引凶yF化仁木方卅z
		else
			EndWindow 3211319

		#\n\nx示白件″″\nx仍户氏y撩ヘ仄化卅仁卅匀切扎匀凶z
		endif
	endif
	Window_yes 
		EndWindow 3211320

		#\n\nx丐木木xR檗互卅中方z

	Window_no
		EndWindow 3211321

		#\n\nx竣互轾中凶日F化仁木方卅
